***передвигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передви́гать</a> (12284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">передви́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredvíg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredvigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to shift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> strélku časóv vperjód (nazád)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the hands of a clock forward/on (back); put a clock forward/on (back)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медленно.html>ме́дленно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">médlenno <b>peredvigája</b> nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slowly dragging one's feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jéle nógi <b>peredvigátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be barely able to drag oneself along [to put one foot in front of the other]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to shift, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнение.html>исполне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> sróki ispolnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change the deadline (for)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздний.html>по́зднюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> na bóleje pózdnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry over; put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́ннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> na bóleje ránnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring/set forward; put ahead</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(to the other position)</i> to move, to transfer</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дви<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>пере-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-двиг-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

***передвинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a> (14058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredvínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to shift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stol nádo <b>peredvínutʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the table should be moved</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> strélku časóv vperjód (nazád)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the hands of a clock forward/on (back); put a clock forward/on (back)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to shift, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнение.html>исполне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> sróki ispolnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change the deadline (for)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздний.html>по́зднюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> na bóleje pózdnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry over; put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́ннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> na bóleje ránnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring/set forward; put ahead</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a> (14933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredélatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to alter, to redo</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alteration, redo
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лку</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdátʹ štó-libo v <b>peredélku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">have smth altered</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюжет.html>сюже́та</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredélka</b> stárovo sjužéta</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">remake</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trouble, mess, fix, scrape

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переделывать.html>переде́лывать</a> (14296)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделывать.html>переде́лывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredélyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></b>)

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лы<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дёр<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>

***передний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передний.html>пере́дний</a> (1937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передний.html>пере́дний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perédnij</span>)
</p>

***передо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>передо</a> (3269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>пе́редо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péredo</span>) <i>+ instrumental case</i> (see <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>in front of, before</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>Передо</a></b> is used instead of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> before <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mnoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мно́ю</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mnóju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and nouns in the instrumental case that start with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ль.html>ль</a></b>, <b>л</b>, <b>м</b>, <b>р</b> + consonant.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предо.html>предо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наперед.html>наперёд</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naperjód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> твор. п.

***передозировка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передозировка.html>передозиро́вка</a> (29732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дозировка.html>дозиро́вка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">doziróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">overdose</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Überdosis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***передохнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передохнувший.html>передохну́вший</a> (8583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнувший.html>передохну́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredoxnúvšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredoxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнувший.html>передохну́вший</a></b>

***передохнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохну́ть</a> (8583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredoxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передыха́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take a break, to have a break, to have a rest, to take a breath <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to have a short rest period in one's work</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гой</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Peredoxní</b> péred dálʹnej dorógoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Take a break</b> before a long journey.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передо́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredóxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передыха́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die off, to extinct, to die in masses <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">especially of animals or when likening people with animals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передо́хнем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My vse zdesʹ <b>peredóxnem</b> bez tebjá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We're all gonna die here without you!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передумавший.html>переду́мавший</a> (6332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передумавший.html>переду́мавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredúmavšij</span>)
</p>
